05073: const toISODate = (d) => {
05074:   if (typeof d === "number" && isFinite(d)) { 
05075:     const dateObj = new Date(Math.round((d - 25569) * 86400000)); 
05076:     return `${dateObj.getUTCFullYear()}-${String(dateObj.getUTCMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(dateObj.getUTCDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`; 
05077:   }
05078:   const s = String(d || "").trim();
05079:   if (!s) return "";
05080:   const isoMatch = s.match(/^(\d{4})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})/);
05081:   if (isoMatch) return `${isoMatch[1]}-${isoMatch[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${isoMatch[3].padStart(2,'0')}`;
05082:   const zhMatch = s.match(/^(\d{4})年\s*(\d{1,2})月\s*(\d{1,2})日?/);
05083:   if (zhMatch) return `${zhMatch[1]}-${zhMatch[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${zhMatch[3].padStart(2,'0')}`;

13683:   const normalizeCell=v=>{
13684:     if(v===null||v===undefined||v===''||(typeof v==='number'&&!Number.isFinite(v)))return '';
13685:     if(v instanceof Date)return v.toISOString();

13689:   const exportViaSheetJS=(sheets,filename)=>{
13690:     if(!window.XLSX?.utils?.book_new)return false;
13691:     const wb=window.XLSX.utils.book_new();
13692:     for(const s of sheets){
13693:       const aoa=[(s.headers||[]).map(normalizeCell),...(s.dataRows||[]).map(row=>(row||[]).map(normalizeCell))];
13694:       const ws=window.XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(aoa);
13695:       if(aoa.length&&aoa[0].length){ws['!autofilter']={ref:window.XLSX.utils.encode_range({s:{r:0,c:0},e:{r:Math.max(0,aoa.length-1),c:aoa[0].length-1}})};ws['!freeze']={xSplit:0,ySplit:1};}
13696:       const widths=(s.headers||[]).map((h,i)=>{let max=String(h??'').length;for(const row of (s.dataRows||[]).slice(0,2000))max=Math.max(max,String(normalizeCell(row?.[i])).length);return{wch:Math.min(50,Math.max(10,max+2))};});
13697:       ws['!cols']=widths;
13698:       window.XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,ws,cleanSheetName(s.sheetName));
13699:     }
13700:     window.XLSX.writeFile(wb,filename,{compression:true});

13702:   };
